\par 
\par WAR OF THE WORLDS
\par 
\par }\pard \ql \li0\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin0\itap0\pararsid15622085 {\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 Naven Bradford
\par }{\f2\fs20\insrsid3170742 June 16, 2001}{\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 
\par 
\par FADE IN:
\par 
\par EXT. MARS SURFACE--DAY
\par 
\par The landscape is a deep, sandy red as we move across the near-barren landscape. There is no sign of life, but a few rocks and ridges line the desert surface. Then, at a brilliant speed, we move up through the clouds, then, as a rocket ship would do, we bu
rst through the Martian atmosphere and into the void of space. 
\par 
\par In the distance, a tiny blue sphere grows to a tremendous size, and majestically reveals itself to be none other than planet Earth in all its glory. Within a few moments, the planet goes from being a glowing celestial body, to...
\par 
\par INT. CLASS ROOM--DAY
\par 
\par ...a poster. It is hung in an ordinary high school science class room. Students sit bored, some asleep, as CLAYTON FORRESTER, early 30\rquote s, writes complicated equations on the chalkboard. There als}{\f2\fs20\insrsid16598682 o seem}{
\f2\fs20\insrsid813511  to be two poorly-drawn diagrams of two planets.
\par 
\par Several students snicker and joke silently as Clayton speaks.
\par 
\par }\pard \ql \li3220\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin3220\itap0\pararsid15622085 {\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 CLAYTON
\par }\pard \ql \li1420\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin1420\itap0\pararsid15622085 {\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 So, by that we can }{\f2\fs20\insrsid16598682 assume}{\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 
 that the probability, while not exact, is that this phenomenon, if that is what you\rquote d call it, will not occur for another...
\par }\pard \ql \li0\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin0\itap0\pararsid15622085 {\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 
\par His voice tapers off as he sees SANCHEZ and PHILLIP, sporting hip jackets and beanies, whisper to each other near the back of the class.
\par 
\par }\pard \ql \li3220\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin3220\itap0\pararsid15622085 {\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 CLAYTON (CON\rquote T)
\par }\pard \ql \li1420\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin1420\itap0\pararsid15622085 {\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 ...few thousand years.
\par }\pard \ql \li0\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin0\itap0\pararsid15622085 {\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 
\par Beat.
\par 
\par Raises his voice.
\par 
\par }\pard \ql \li3220\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin3220\itap0\pararsid15622085 {\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 CLAYTON

\par

\par All eyes turn to Sanchez as he looks around, thinking of something to say. Stuttering, he speaks, smiles innocently.
\par

\par Students break out in befuddled laughter as SANCHEZ sits silently, not sure what to do. Clayton sighs.
\par 
\par INT. OFFICE--DAY
\par 
\par Clayton sits at a desk in what appears to be a teachers\rquote  lounge. He is alone, grading papers. 
\par 
\par FOCUS ON the papers. Many are below average grades, many others are marked with FAIL stamps. A radio plays a news broadcasts in the b.g.
\par 
\par }\pard \ql \li3220\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin3220\itap0\pararsid15622085 {\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 BROADCASTER (V.O.)
\par }\pard \ql \li1420\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin1420\itap0\pararsid15622085 {\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 ...barred by serious electrical disturbances that appear to have manifested from nowhere, thousands are without power in various cities...
\par }\pard \ql \li0\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin0\itap0\pararsid15622085 {\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 
\par Clayton clicks the radio off.
\par 
\par CUT TO:
\par 
\par EXT. SALTSBURG--DUSK
\par 
\par WIDE SHOT, establishing.
\par 
\par It is a picturesque little town, the kind of to
wn where everybody knows everybody. A large church sits in the middle of the shop district, a sort of landmark, while a few rows of little houses lie on the outskirts. There is a single bridge leading out of the town, which is surrounded with forestry. 

\par 
\par SUPER: SALTSBURG, PENNSLYVANIA
\par 
\par EXT. CLAYTON\rquote S HOUSE--NIGHT
\par 
\par His house is one of several on a street that appears to be sloping downwards into the center of town. It is two stories, at least thirty years old, and nearly identical (in structure) to all the others on his street.
\par 
\par Clayton moves around the side of the house carrying several garbage bags. He dumps them into cans.
\par 
\par INT. KITCHEN, CLAYTON\rquote S HOUSE--NIGHT
\par 
\par Clayton walks into the kitchen and starts for the refrigerator. SARAH, only 7-years old stands on a stool over the sink, washing dishes.
\par 
\par Clayton stand}{\f2\fs20\insrsid16598682 s}{\f2\fs20\insrsid813511  up from digging through the fridge and pops open a beer, after a sip, looks at his watch, then to SARAH.
\par 
\par }\pard \ql \li3220\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin3220\itap0\pararsid15622085 {\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 CLAYTON
\par }\pard \ql \li1420\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin1420\itap0\pararsid15622085 {\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 Sarah, bed time.
\par }\pard \ql \li0\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin0\itap0\pararsid15622085 {\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 
\par She protests.
\par 
\par }\pard \ql \li3220\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin3220\itap0\pararsid15622085 {\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 SARAH
\par }\pard \ql \li1420\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin1420\itap0\pararsid15622085 {\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 I\rquote m not done.

\par }\pard \ql \li0\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin0\itap0\pararsid15622085 {\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 
\par With a slight moan, she marches out of the kitchen.
\par 
\par EXT. BACK YARD, CLAYTON\rquote S HOUSE--NIGHT
\par 
\par Clayton sits upon a picnic table, his beer at his side and a pair of binoculars in his hands. All is silent but the sounds of crickets and distant birds. The sky is full of stars. He occasionally swaps his beer with the binoculars.
\par 
\par SARAH surprises him.

\par EXT. JENKINS FARM--DAY
\par 
\par Finally, Clayton reaches the end of the parade. On the edge of the town is a farm, and in the field, not more than a football field\rquote s distan
ce from the silo and barn, is en enormous METEOR. It is stuck in the ground, half-buried; the part sticking up is about thirty-feet tall. Strangely, it doesn\rquote 
t appear to be solid rock, but a strange, silvery-rock covered in dust and debris, creating the illusion of a meteorite.
\par 
\par There is police tape all around the perimeter of the meteor, and several POLICEMEN, but no police cars.
\par 
\par CLAYTON rushes to the front of the crowd, along the police tape, about a hundred feet from the enormous object. He takes out his disposable camera and aims for a picture.

\par The docks separate, and begin to sink, Clayton, along with many other people, are trapped on a quickly-sinking raft of wooden dock.
\par 
\par The third tripod takes to zapping and grabbing people just as its two brothers are. Then, in an instant, all three tripods point to different ferries and ZAP away, incinerating people and setting fire to the decks. They, too, quickly begin to sink. 

\par 
\par Suddenly, a few scared people push by Clayton, knocking him and Sarah into the water.
\par 
\par EXT. UNDER WATER--NIGHT
\par 
\par Under water, Clayton struggles with 
a squirming Sarah, as we can see the entire length of the third, submerged tripod. Metal tentacles reach down into the water and grab people, while lasers rip through, zapping others. Somehow, Clayton and Sarah manage to surface.

\par EXT. RIVER--NIGHT

\par EXT. ROAD TO PITTSBURGH--DAY
\par 
\par The road is deserted, except for the red weed growing everywhere. A large sign sits in the boulevard on the side of the road, it reads \'93WELCOME TO PITTSBURGH,\'94 but is almost }{\f2\fs20\insrsid12671692 illegible}{\f2\fs20\insrsid813511

\par EXT. PITTSBURGH STREETS--DAY
\par 
\par Clayton\rquote s hummer stops suddenly as a crowd of people blocks his way. All the people are apparently trying to get past a military blockade.

\par INT. HUMMER--DAY
\par 
\par Clayton grips the steering wheel tight as a few people in the crowd turn to his car. Suddenly, the window shatters in a spidery web of cracks as people are, out of nowhere, climbing all over his car, yelling, screaming, kicking to get in.
\par 
\par EXT. PITTSBURGH STREETS--DAY
\par 
\par The mob has created a mountain of bodies atop the hummer, chaos makes men animals.
\par 
\par INT. HUMMER--DAY
\par 
\par Clayton struggles to pull out his pistol when suddenly a man\rquote s hand bursts through the driver\rquote s-side window and grabs Clayton by the shoulder. Glass is pushed through his clothes, he writhes in pain and drops his pistol to the floor.
\par 
\par Finally, he reaches down and opens the door.
\par 
\par EXT. PITTSBURGH STREETS--DAY
\par 
\par The driver\rquote s-side door opens and Clayton is pulled out. He is pushed forcefully though the mob and literally thrown to the ground. 
\par

\par 
\par All of this is silenced when we suddenly hear the now-familiar call of a Martian-tripod.
\par 
\par All eyes turn up the street as a 70-foot tall tripod machine stands, staring at the people below. Now, the fighting in the mob becomes more intense, some people take for the streets as the military barrage starts firing wildly.
\par 
\par Clayton lays on the ground, barely able to keep his head up, his nose broken and bleeding.
\par 
\par The tripod moves one leg forward, shakily, then another, before finally, its guns firing, falls onto a nearby building, crushing it.
\par 
\par Everything seems to go silent.
\par

\par Military folk start jogging towards it, random \lquote come on\rquote s\rquote  and such }{\f2\fs20\insrsid12671692 echo}{\f2\fs20\insrsid813511  throughout. Clayton stands upright and grabs the arm of a passing soldier.

\par Curious chatter rises in the silence.
\par 
\par EXT. MITCHEL STREET--DAY
\par 
\par It is much clearer out, not an orange-glow like before.
\par 
\par We see the door to the church open, and several people walk outside.
\par 
\par ZOOM OUT: The head of a Martian-tripod machine lays broken and busted in the middle of the intersection. The legs have crushed a few buildings down the street, but the church was just missed.
\par 
\par People gather curiously around the wrecked tripod head. 
\par 
\par Suddenly, a circular door appears to open near the bottom of the tripod head. Orange liquid spills out as people, especially soldiers, gather around for a closer look. 
\par 
\par Eerily, a veiny, Martian arm reaches out, struggling, and grabs the lip of the opening. We hear a wheezing coming from inside the tripod. The arm, suddenly starts to stiffen, and its }{\f2\fs20\insrsid12671692 gloomy}{\f2\fs20\insrsid813511 
 blue color turns to a stale gray. It stops, dead.
\par 
\par A soldier grabs the arm, lifts it, and drops it.
\par

\par EXT. SPACE
